Instructions for sharing KeyShotXR

Below is your KeyShotXR. To view the KeyShotXR by itself open the pc60= x8.510.html file in the pc60x8.510 folder.

 

Uploading to and displaying on your website:

Upload the 'pc60x8.510' folder with all of its contents to your webs= erver. Copy (Ctrl-C/Cmd-C) and Paste (Ctrl-V/Cmd-V) the code below to your webpage.

[Code]: 

<div style=3D"max-width: 800px; max-height: 800px;">
  <div style=3D=
"left: 0px; width: 100%; height: 0px; position: relative; padding-bottom: 1=
00%; overflow: hidden;">
    <iframe src=3D"pc60x8.510.html"
                 allowfullscreen
                 style=3D"position: absolute; t=
op: 0px; left: 0px; height: 100%; width: 1px; min-width: 100%; *width: 100%=
;"
                 frameborder=3D"0"
                 scrolling=3D"no">
    </iframe>
  </div>
</div>

If you share your KeyShotXR via email, send the entire zipped 'pc60x= 8.510' folder to the recipient(s).
